                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="716">
                        Comfortable private bedroom in a nicely refurbished home, nestled in a quiet, convenient and safe little pocket of Central Phoenix. There is plenty of free street parking in front of our home, but public transportation (bus, light rail, plus taxi) are all within a 2 block walk, (and then of course there's Uber/Lyft too...) so renting a car while staying with us becomes optional, not mandatory. Starbucks, Target, Walmart, Costco, Walgreens, Movie Theater, restaurants, etc...are 3 blocks away.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="717">
                        We have a roomy 1800 sq. ft. home with extra bedrooms that we really enjoy renting out on AirBnB, mostly to meet other interesting travelers, and also to help fund our own travel/exploration bug. Our home is centrally located in a safe and quiet lower-to-mid-income family-friendly neighborhood in the convenient "mid-town" section of Phoenix, has plenty of free parking, and is only 2 blocks away from the Montebello Transit Station (including both a bus hub, and our Light Rail commuter train), which will take you to/from the Airport (11mi), Convention Center (5.1 mi), Downtown (4mi), Spring Training and other sporting events (varies: 1.5 to 22 mi), Tempe / Mill Ave / ASU (17mi), Scottsdale (11mi), Glendale (5.7mi), and so on. We are less than 5 minutes from great walking and biking on Central Avenue, and hiking or mountain biking at Squaw Peak Park or North Mountain Park, as well as tennis courts, basketball courts, and more...are all within walking/biking distance of our home. This listing is for a private, individually-keyed 12' x 13' guestroom with it's own closet, lamp, ceiling fan, windows to let in lots of natural light, top-down/bottom-up blinds, individual air purifier, as well as a humidifier. We love a clean home, so we have our home professionally cleaned every 10 days, so the shared-space stays tidy. Also included is access to our shared-space remodeled and spacious living room, nicely decorated with photographic travel art, and furnished with a large and comfy sectional leather sofa, a refurbished dining area with a Pub-height Gathering table (seats 8) and a (shared) nicely remodeled Travertine-tiled bathroom w/ full bath tub / shower, already stocked with shampoo, conditioner, towels, and hair dryer, so you can pack light. Feel free to whip up a meal or two in our large and newly remodeled "galley-style" kitchen while you're here...and unless you're a professional chef, we have all the kitchen equipment you'd ever need, I think. (maybe even if you ARE a professional chef, lol). We are only 2 blocks from the Montebello Light Rail station and bus depot, which will take you to/from the airport, downtown, the Convention Center, and ASU/ Tempe, so having a car is not at all necessary. Here's an idea of all the fun places you will find along our Light Rail line: search: "RailLife Phoenix" We're both major "people people". Kevin works from the house, but is quiet, and allows you the freedom to come and go as you please, through your own entrance. Alisa has a teenage son in Flagstaff, and splits her time between there and here. When we get the chance, we love to roam the planet (by Jeep or by plane, or via our 4x4 Overlanding (RV) vehicle we're building...). Even if we're out on the road traveling, we're always available for advice in person or by phone/text about great restaurants, directions, can't-miss attractions, etc. Compared to a single-room hotel or motel room, not only is this bedroom and living room HUGE, with lots of room to spread out, but there's also some additional space for an air mattress we can set up if you need room for 3 total guests (additional cost for the third person). Sheets, blankets, and pillows are all provided. Did I mention it is HUGE? Lots more space for you and your friends or family than a hotel room would have! We are big believers in the "Make Yourself At Home" philosophy, and we want you to be comfortable! You are welcome to use anything in the house that you need. The kitchen and bathroom are fully stocked for you. You can even have us run a load of laundry for you for just $10/load washed and dried...enough to cover our costs and to fund the expensive washer repairs. If you are coming to Phoenix to explore the city, a quick drive from our place will get you almost anywhere town and the 20 surrounding cities that make up the "Valley Metro Area". We are happy to help you plan your adventures if you would like suggestions. From white water rafting and golf lessons, to wine tastings and museums, (not to mention the GREAT diverse restaurant selection nearby!) we have found a lot of fun things to do in the Phoenix area! If you are going to be traveling around the Southwest after your time in Phoenix, you can feel free to leave bigger bags here (locked away in a secure storage) and use our place as your home-base. San Diego, LA, Las Vegas, and the beaches of Rocky Point Mexico are all about 4-6 hours away. The Grand Canyon, Sedona, White Mountains, and AZ's wine country are 1-4 hours. Take your carry-on, and leave the big stuff here, while you explore! We have been to almost every corner of the state, so if you want to know the hidden treasures, we would be happy to tell you our favorite places to visit. We have a wide variety of sports and camping equipment to get you outside and enjoying the AZ scenery during your visit. Some of the items you are welcome to use for an additional cost while staying with us are: - Mountain bikes (local use only) - Water bottles and day-hiking backpacks - Camping equipment (tent, sleeping bags, air mattresses, camping cookware, lanterns) - Overnight backpacking backpacks - And more! If you have any questions on the listing, or Phoenix in general, just send us a message. We look forward to getting to know you!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="718">
                        What you WON'T see in our neighborhood: perfectly manicured lawns, perfectly painted exteriors of every home, a Mercedes in every driveway, gated communities, gilded streets of gold, or anything remotely resembling the aesthetics of either Scottsdale or Beverly Hills, lol. What you WILL see is an older, quiet, lower-to-middle-income neighborhood, with lots of owner-occupied homes, most of them fairly well taken care of. Some of our neighbors have owned here for many decades, and other younger families have recently purchased theirs from fix-and-flippers, who have nicely revamped portions our neighborhood for us during the 2008-2010 downturn. We attend neighborhood meetings, and keep each other up to date on the Nextdoor app, which is essentially a social sharing site for neighborhoods...which brings all of our neighbors a little bit closer. We know almost all of our nextdoor neighbors by name, and the average age here is probably 45 or 50 years old, so it's quiet during the night, with no college parties or obnoxious neighbors. You'll hear the "clickety-clack" of the light rail commuter train switching tracks a block away, but only if you're paying attention. :-)
                       </div>

                        <li data-reactid="728"><p data-reactid="729">Great place to stay, especially if you don't have a car. The apartment is about 2.5 blocks from the very last stop on the line (handy to know you cannot miss the stop!) on the light rail. Kevin and Alisa were so welcoming and helpful. The shared bathroom is just across from both rooms so very handy. There's also a guest living room and separate guest fridge which is great. I never cooked there but their kitchen is huge and well equipped. The bedroom is super quiet and has everything you could need including all different types of pillows and tons of towels. There's a huge shopping mall just 3 blocks away with a Target with a huge frozen and fresh produce (including organic) selection. So the location really is handy. There's a cinema round the corner there so for any night your're not energized to go out, that's a good option. I was able to visit a lot of places downtown just using the light rail including the Phoenix Art Museum (great Warhol exhibition right now), Phoenix Public Market. For further away, I'd recommend a car for a day or two. Handy hints for future guests: the Desert Botanical Garden is free the second Tuesday of every month (I happened to go that day by accident) Phoenix Art Museum is free every Wednesday from 3pm to 9pm except any special exhibition (Warhol is worth the $8) I also went to one of Kevin's recommendations for wine tastings, Postino's, also easily accessible from the light rail at Indian School Road stop. Fantastic wine selection and good cheese board, friendly atmosphere for anyone to go solo or in a group. Kevin was so helpful and responsive with suggestions on where to go and what to do. I would definitely recommend a day trip to Sedona and Red Rock Canyon. The drive is long and I'd recommend a tour than trying to do this yourself. I couldn't find many tours leaving from Phoenix so I recommend DetoursAZ ((SENSITIVE CONTENTS HIDDEN) them). For transportation without renting, sign up for Uber and Lyft. With Lyft I was given 10 rides for $5 for the first 15 days; ideal if you are here on vacation. Tip: get a car at least for half your time here. I booked with Enterprise on Camelback Road, about a mile away, but they still picked me up and rental was about $40 USD after everything was included. If you are a US citizen (I am not), there’s something called Rapid Rides where you can rent privately owned cars and they can even deliver them. Was not able to try out the service but for a modest compact car like a Ford Focus, the daily rate was $28. Great place overall - highly recommended!!!</p><span data-reactid="730">Sarah</span><span data-reactid="731">2015-06-14T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="985">
                        Modernism meets Spanish revival in this beautifully restored home in the Encanto Historic District. Meticulously restored - everything is brand new but with respect for the homes original character. Our home is located in a quiet, safe neighborhood while also close to hip restaurants, nightlife, and minutes to downtown. This home as been a very special second home for us and we welcome all - we will never decline a guest based on race, color, religion or sexual orientation.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="986">
                        This home is ideal for creatives of any kind - architects, photographers, designers, really anyone with an eye for beautiful design. The space has been remodeled from floor to ceiling and is in stunning, like new condition. Kids like it too, with a huge backyard, and big lawn. The backyard has two lounge chairs (under their own shape canopy) with ottomans, ideal for relaxing outside, watching the kids, and enjoying a cappuccino in the morning or a glass of wine at night. The brand new BBQ is close by as well. The home is also well equipped for business travelers with self check-in, 70MB/sec wireless internet and an AirPrint printer. An Apple lightning charger cable is located at the master bedroom night stand. FedEx drop off is available 1/2 mile up the road at Safeway.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="987">
                        Encanto-Palmcroft is an attractive and desirable place to live. Many residents are renovating, restoring and remodeling their homes with enthusiasm and flair. Neighbors pride themselves and work hard to maintain the neighborhood spirit that has developed. Numerous hip and award winning restaurants are opening up and giving the area a modern, current feel. We are close to Encanto Park, Encanto Golf Course, downtown, the funky Melrose District, and the entire Midtown/Central Avenue corridor.

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1713">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1714">
                        This large bedroom with queen iron bed is located in the heart of the Melrose district known for its vintage and antique boutiques. Around corner from Gridbike share.85 restaurants within 1 mile and 15 min walk to lightrail
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1715">
                        Central Phoenix has a lot of charm, but doesn't always have a lot of space. We've got both! This spacious room can be your home-base in the heart of the Melrose district. Need a second bedroom for your party? See our other listing at the same address. Our split-plan home means everyone has full privacy. You have your own full bathroom in the guest section. Plenty of closet space means you can unpack and make Melrose Manor your home away from home. We've even got 2 kitties for you to love on if you're missing your fur babies! Room has charming world traveler decor with a wrought-iron queen bed. Bed had firm support with a pillow top. Black-out blinds mean you can sleep as late as you need to without letting our bright Arizona sun in during those winter visits. Room has a ceiling fan if you love a light breeze while you sleep as much as we do.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1716">
                        Everybody's peanut butter and jealous that we live in the Melrose district, and we're so excited about sharing all it has to offer with you! Melrose is known for its quirky vintage and antique stores (Its dangerous being this close. Seriously). There are 85 restaurants within one mile of the house and include the hottest restaurants in the Valley like Southern Rail, Hula's, and Gallo Blanco. Lux, one of the most popular coffee shops (with a bar) is less than a mile, as is Changing Hands Bookstore (which also has a bar). Steele Indian School Park- the Central Park of Phoenix- is less than a mile away, and the Heard Museum (3miles), Phoenix Museum (3.1 miles) are a short ride on the lightrail or a bike ride away. There is a Grid Bike Share rack right around the corner from us, with over 35 racks within the central corridor to make enjoying our 75F January days even better.
                       </div>

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2217">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2218">
                        Private Apartment with separate entry in Heart of downtown arts &amp; culture in beautiful Historic Willo district. Walking Score is 77!!! Walk 1 block to Central Avenue to Phoenix Art Center, Heard Museum, Light Rail 2 blocks &amp; numerous restaurants, coffee shops &amp; nightlife. Parking on street. Enjoy relaxing on any of 3 lovely patios. As your Hosts we provide lots of goodies to eat and drink and extra touches to make you comfortable and so, welcome home!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2219">
                        Home is in Historic Cottage Living district. This is a large 2 room apt in lower level of our home with high ceilings and an open feel, with full banks of window wells allowing great indirect light with shade cover &amp; private entry. 1st room has a full bed and the 2nd room has a full futon and features a completly outfitted kitchen including stove and oven so guests may cook. The apt. comfortably fits 4 who share sleeping. We can take more if necessary with discussion first as there's a blow up queen airbed. Extra charges per person apply over 2 guests, including children. There's a straight flight (14 steps) down to the apartment which are to code and have a sturdy handrail.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2220">
                        Quiet, friendly, historic beauty. It is bike and walk friendly. We are centrally located in Phoenix art- focused areas with several theaters, museums, symphony &amp; opera. Walk or ride the light rail! Grid rental bikes available just down the street and there are designated paths through the neighborhood and into downtown &amp; throughout the Valley and Mountain trails. There are great places in walking distance to eat/drink including Starbucks, and from the light rail! ( our favorite place is Oven &amp; Vine one stop up on the Light Rail, or walking distance a few blocks!) Guests can take a short walk to the Phoenix Art Museum and the Heard Indian Art Museum (both have delightful lunch cafes!), to the Light Rail and Arizona Opera House, which has special offerings depending on the day. Talking Stick Arena with sports and concerts is just within 2 miles on the light rail with its own stop. The area is convenient to I-10, the 51 North, the 202 East and great for connecting to most Spring Training areas by freeway or Light Rail/metro transportation. Take a day trip to Northern AZ to see old mining towns like Jerome, or spend a day in red rocks in Sedona! Phoenix is a great launching place to take a trip to the Grand Canyon! And we'll keep the lights burning at home for your welcome back!
                       </div>

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2500">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2501">
                        Clean, private and spacious, this private guest house is located only a few minutes from all the downtown action and also in close proximity to some of the best food and coffee spots. This quiet studio will be perfect for couples, solo adventurers, and business travelers.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2502">
                        Perfectly cozy, clean and private. This private guest house has its own garage, entrance and backyard space fenced off and locked. We took care to try and keep the charm of this historic house, while giving it a modern look. It's a larger studio space with everything you need to enjoy your stay. The kitchen has a mini fridge, toaster oven, hot plate for cooking with one pan or one pot and microwave for your basic needs and cups, plates and other necessities. There is one large space with a comfy queen mattresses, couch, dresser, TV and dining space for 2. The bathroom has a shower. When you walk into the guest house, it's open, light and welcoming. We want to make sure that you feel right at home. You have the use of the entire studio and can enjoy the cooler weather in your own backyard. The garage can only fit a small or mid sized car. Please note you have to enter the home through the garage and the garage is located at the back of the house through an alley.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2503">
                        Our neighborhood is part of the historic district and that means that us and our neighbors take pride in our community. Our neighborhood is quiet and we have families and couples that have lived in the area for a long time. We are also very close to Encanto park which has tons of space for hanging out, walking, kid activities, rides and more! We aren't too far from the monorail, which will give you easy access downtown and through Central Phoenix.
                       </div>
